Important News

Chiang Kai-shek 88

Telegrams Wang to Persuade Him Not to Resign Hastily 89

And Sends Personnel to Shanghai to Persuade Him

Hankou Correspondence, After Chiang Kai-shek arrived in Hankou on June 28, he went to Xun twice in the middle, and is now supervising the suppression of the Red Army in various provinces to thoroughly clear all the bandits. However, on the 6th, he received a telegram from the President of the Executive Yuan, Wang Jingwei, resigning. Wang also asked Chiang to return to Beijing to preside over the Central Political Conference. That night, Chiang immediately sent an urgent telegram to Mr. Wang, earnestly urging him to stay. The general idea of the original telegram was: Since we have all come to face the national crisis together, no matter what difficulties there are now, we must bear the responsibility together and bravely overcome the difficulties. We must not have the idea of resigning hastily at a time when the national crisis is becoming more serious. We hope that you will return to Beijing immediately and preside over the affairs of the Yuan as usual. At the same time, he telegraphed Chairman Lin in Guling, asking him to persuade him to stay, and separately telegraphed He Yingqin in Nanjing, Wu Techeng and Song Ziwen in Shanghai to jointly persuade him to stay. On the afternoon of the 7th, Chiang also summoned Wang Shijie, the president of Wuhan University, to his official residence in Yihua Village, and instructed him to telegraph Shanghai to ask Cai Yuanpei to persuade Wang to return to Beijing to avoid a lack of responsible person in the central government. After receiving the instruction, Wang immediately telegraphed Cai to persuade him to stay. The telegram said: Mr. Wang resigned, and no one can succeed him. The League of Nations meeting is approaching, and the central government should not be shaken. Mr. Jieshi specifically asked me to ask you to do your best to persuade Mr. Wang to return to Beijing no matter what. I hereby convey this to you. On the 8th, the Shanghai telegram conveyed that Wang's intention to resign had not been dispelled. Chiang then sent Wuhan University professor Zhou Gengsheng as a representative to Shanghai to persuade him in person. Zhou took the Jiangyu ship east on the evening of the 8th. When he passed through Beijing, he would invite Tang Youren to go to Shanghai together, because Chiang had no intention of returning to Beijing for the time being. (August 8)

Northeast 90

General Mobilization of Righteous Armies 91

Japanese troops in all areas are adopting a defensive posture. A dispatch from Beiping states that, according to sources within the Volunteer Army, the various Volunteer Armies of Liaoning and Ning provinces have begun a general offensive against the Japanese army. Shenyang and Jinzhou are both showing signs of wavering. Reports received over the past few days are as follows:

The Fourth Route Volunteer Army of Zheng Guilin on the Fengshan Line, in Jinxi, has been fighting the Japanese army in the vicinity of Suizhong and Xingcheng along the railway line for days. They have dismantled four or five miles of the pseudo-Fengshan railway, at a location two *li* west of Lianshan Station. The Japanese armored train stationed at the station fired upon them. The pseudo-Fengshan railway train arriving at Shanhaiguan was delayed by four hours. The Eighth Division Volunteer Army of Ma Zidan in Yixian on the northern route has also been engaged in fierce fighting with the Japanese army near Chaoyang Temple and Liulongtai Village for days. The independent regiment of Li Haifeng, in conjunction with the various units of Liu Chunqi, has been advancing fiercely from Hongluoxian in Jinxi since the 3rd, intending to encircle Jinzhou. Great panic prevails in that area. Volunteer Armies in Goubangzi, Qingduizi, and Dahushan are also engaging the Japanese army. The First Division Volunteer Army of Wang Shu on the northern route has occupied Tongliao. Traffic on the branch line of the pseudo-Fengshan railway has been suspended. The Lao Beifeng unit at Dahushan, Dongbaiqibao, and Raoyang River has also risen up to fight the Japanese army.

South Manchuria Railway: The Volunteer Army on the South Manchuria Railway has destroyed much of the railway line. Traffic on the South Manchuria Railway has been suspended. On the branch line from Yingkou to Goubangzi, between Tianzhuangtai and Panshan, a large force of the Volunteer Army attacked Majiayingzi, twelve *li* north of Yingkou from Tianzhuangtai on the 5th, capturing a Japanese tank. Twenty *li* from Shenyang, large forces of the Volunteer Army are concealed in the sorghum fields and have begun attacking the Japanese army. The main force of the Volunteer Army is advancing towards Shenyang. Fierce fighting is expected in Shenyang in the coming days. Regarding the Jinzhou-Chaoyang Line, the Japanese previously used the arrest of Ishimoto Kenshiro as a pretext to station considerable troops at Chaoyang Temple Station. It is rumored that Japanese Lieutenant General Muto will take command of the Jinxi military operations to rescue Ishimoto. Traffic on the Jinzhou-Chaoyang Line has been suspended for several days. Moreover, a certain party has released detailed information on the fierce fighting between the various Volunteer Armies and the enemy,

as follows:

Haicheng: (1) After receiving orders to operate on schedule, our army of the First Route began preparations. On the night of the first day, it mobilized various units to positions north, west, and south of Haicheng Station on the South Manchuria Railway, launching an encirclement attack. Around midnight, they made contact with the Japanese garrison stationed there, resulting in fierce fighting. After about half an hour, the vanguard of our army had approached the station to within about two hundred paces, but due to the presence of electric fences set up by the Japanese army, our army could not penetrate further. (2) In order to cut off Japanese reinforcements from Liaoyang and Dashiqiao, and to implement a policy of terror, our forces divided into two detachments to harass Nantai, about twenty *li* south of Haicheng, and Liujiatun, about twenty *li* north, creating disturbances. Contact was made at dawn on the 2nd, and the Japanese army suffered heavy casualties. They have apparently requested assistance from Liaoyang and Dashiqiao. (3) On the 2nd

in the afternoon, our army changed its attack direction with full force, attacking the Japanese railway concession, the base of the Japanese army in Haicheng. They cooperated in the attack from the north and south starting at 8:00 PM, immediately breaking in and engaging in chaotic street fighting with the local garrison, puppet police, and Japanese police. Japanese women and children within the concession fled in droves. Our army was ordered not to harm them. Our army's momentum was strong, and the Japanese artillery units retreated in two groups. Japanese reinforcements from Dashiqiao have arrived and are now in formal contact with our army, currently engaged in fierce fighting.

Liaoyang: Our army, under the command of Wang Quansheng, consisting of 5,000 men, moved from the Dashaling and Huangniwa areas on the 29th, appearing and disappearing intermittently. At dawn on the 31st, they officially went into action, burning a railway bridge on the Japanese South Manchuria Railway, cutting its long-distance telephone lines, and engaging Japanese sentries. They planned to destroy the Japanese water source in Shoushan, the iron mine in Anshan, and the Japanese station in Liaoyang. According to intelligence, Japanese military police, police, and puppet police in Anshan, Shoushan, Zhangtaizi, and Shilihe, along with local Japanese veterans, have set up electric fences and sandbags around the local water source, mine, bank, substation, and

station and are on guard all night.

Yingkou: The Lao Beifeng unit, numbering about 5,000, launched a powerful night attack on the old urban area of Yingkou from Niujiatun at 4:00 AM on the first day. They charged in under the cover of darkness and engaged in battle with the Japanese military police and puppet police. The sounds of gunfire were intense and the sound of artillery fire could be heard throughout the city. The Japanese were extremely alarmed by the intensity of the National Salvation Army's attack. Japanese banks, shops, and Japanese civilians and soldiers throughout the city have sent their women and children to ships on the Liao River for safety, and have set up electric fences, maintaining a serious state of alert.

Panyang: A unit of our army is lying in wait in the Sujiatun area, waiting for an opportunity to act. On the 2nd, they arrested two Japanese Manchuria Railway inspectors, marking the beginning of our army's operations. Our army plans to attack Shenyang in the near future and has already made considerable preparations on the southern and eastern sides of the northeast. Plainclothes units have been deployed inside the city to act as internal support. Action will begin soon.

Changchun: At around 7:00 PM on the 30th, according to intelligence from the puppet police, approximately 1,000 infantry and cavalry of the Wang Delin National Salvation Army suddenly appeared in the southern part of Changchun as an advance guard. The main force of about 8,000 was about forty *li* behind. Judging by their direction of movement, they appeared to be planning an attack on Changchun. The Japanese military police and puppet military police in Changchun are now cooperating in maintaining security. In addition, the Changchun air squadron dispatched a light bomber carrying bombs to Nanling to bomb the local National Salvation Army. Martial law has been declared in Changchun, and many so-called important figures of the puppet organization have taken refuge at the Japanese station.

Traitors 92

Plot to Disturb Tianjin Fails 93

Sun Yichen Succeeds Liu Xuegu Tianjin Dispatch: After the *hanjian* Liu Xuegu was arrested on the 5th, Wang Yimin, the director of the Public Security Bureau, personally escorted him to Beiping, removing a hidden danger for the region, to the great satisfaction of the people. However, Sun Yichen, the deputy leader of the plainclothes squad (Sun had served as the Tianjin *daoyin* when Chu Yupu was the military governor of Zhili), was extremely shocked. On the one hand, he reported to the military police and constabulary authorities of the Japanese concession, requesting a protest to the Public Security Bureau, and on the other hand, he searched for spies within the plainclothes squad. As a result, the Japanese police station issued a major demerit to the patrolman on duty on Suma Street, Shianli, for failing to provide adequate protection, and requested the Japanese consulate to protest to the municipal government. However, as there was no corroborating evidence, the municipal government has not yet received a letter of protest. As for Sun Yichen's investigation of the plainclothes squad, it is said that he discovered several undercover special agents (this is the secret term for special forces), and immediately subjected them to harsh interrogation. Their subsequent whereabouts are unknown. Some say they have already been put to death. Yesterday (the 6th) evening at 6:00 PM, Sun convened an emergency meeting and decided to launch a riot at 9:00 PM on the 7th, and notified the armies that had been won over to launch a simultaneous uprising, and presumptuously claimed that they would occupy Beiping and destroy Zhang Xueliang's base. The Japanese military in Tianjin naturally strongly supported this plan. However, at 10:00 PM that night, the Japanese consulate suddenly urged the Japanese military to prevent troublemakers from causing disturbances in the Japanese concession. The Japanese Resident Association also knew that the plainclothes squad was weak and could not succeed, and advocated caution. The Japanese military then summoned Sun for questioning at midnight, rigorously questioning whether he was confident in the riot. Sun said he was confident and cited so-and-so brigade commander and so-and-so regimental commander who had signed written pledges to participate in the anti-Zhang movement. The Japanese military said that since he was confident, he could operate outside the Japanese concession, and the Japanese military would provide covert assistance. Sun, listening to this advice, could not help but feel apprehensive and decided to postpone the launch. However, yesterday (the 6th), the Japanese army suddenly prepared 10,000 sacks and transported sand and soil to empty houses outside Qiangzi River on Fukushima Street and stockpiled them, and also prepared a large quantity of electrical wiring material. Perhaps the Japanese army is actively planning to assist Sun's riot. (7th)

Local Dispatches

Songjiang 94

The Dispute over Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Continues: The auction of tobacco and alcohol licenses and the tobacco and alcohol business license tax were previously the subject of disputes between the provincial and central governments, leaving merchants at a loss. Subsequently, the Ministry of Finance adopted a bidding system. It is said that a certain Yao has won the bid to manage the tobacco and alcohol license tax for this county and Qingjin County for 12,500 yuan. Unexpectedly, the county government received a telegram from the Department of Finance stating that the tobacco and alcohol license tax in this province would be managed by the province starting from July 1, and collection would be implemented, ordering all counties to assist. However, it is recently heard that many tobacco and alcohol merchants in various counties are still mostly waiting and seeing, and are not going to the various provincial bureaus to pay their taxes. This is partly due to the merchants' attempts to be opportunistic, but it also reflects the lack of assistance from the county magistrates. Provincial tax collection and provincial management should be consistent in name and reality. Before the method has been changed, the province should collect the tax according to the original plan. A telegram should be sent again ordering them to comply with repeated orders and provide sincere assistance, and to inform all tobacco and alcohol merchants to promptly go to the various provincial bureaus to pay their taxes according to regulations. If they still dare to resist and delay, they should be strictly pursued and collected, and the county should reissue a public notice to inform them and avoid self-destruction of their businesses, etc. The dispute over tobacco and alcohol business license tax between the ministry and the province is in full swing.

Suzhou 95

Gao Liao Suffers Poverty and Illness in Prison: In the case of the former San Francisco Deputy Consul Gao Ying and his wife trafficking in opium, Gao Ying has already served his sentence and been released from prison. His wife, Liao Suqiu, was originally sentenced to four years, but the sentence was reduced to two years on appeal. Now, after discounting the number of days in custody, the sentence is about to expire. She is awaiting release after the fine of 4,000 yuan is paid. However, Liao is suffering from poverty and illness, and her relatives and friends are ashamed of her. Her husband, Gao Ying, has also not sent any news for a long time. It is feared that it will be difficult to raise the fine.

Zhong Tingxi et al. Detained on Suspicion of Communism: Zhong Tingxi and five others from the station stevedores union were previously detained by Zhu Yanliang, the supervisor of the county party headquarters, in conjunction with the Public Security Bureau, on suspicion of communism, and sent to the High Court. Yesterday (the 9th), prosecutor Zhu Wenzhao investigated the case. As a result, Liu Jinkun, Xu Fangfu, Li Hengquan, and Huang Qiaobiao were found to be less involved and were released on bail in court. Zhong was returned to custody to await trial in the criminal court.

Wuxi 96

Changshu Chamber of Commerce Discusses Business Tax: The chambers of commerce of Wujin, Wuxi, Yixing, Jiangyin, and Jingjiang counties in the old Changzhou prefecture held a meeting at the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce yesterday afternoon to discuss the business tax issue. Representatives from various counties had arrived in advance. Since the promulgation of the Suzhou Provincial Provisional Regulations on Business Tax, all industries in Wuxi have complained that the tax rate has been increased to twice or one and a half times the old regulations. At a time when the market is in decline and business is depressed, they feel it is unbearable. They have put forward various opinions. Industries such as silk and cloth, paper, sauce and wine, and tea have requested that the tax be temporarily levied at 2/1000, the same as the grain and flour business tax. The Rice Industry Association argues that the industry holds a *yatie* (license) and has traditionally been a mix of retail and wholesale, or retail-only, purely adjusting agriculture and commerce, and is not a department store business. They request that the tax be levied based on capital, similar to the banking industry. All of these have been submitted to the general meeting, which has decided to ask the Chamber of Commerce Federation to argue the case based on reason. In addition, the chambers of commerce of the various counties under the Suzhou prefecture held a meeting in Suzhou on the afternoon of the 8th. As a result, it was decided to proceed in accordance with the six points decided by the Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation on the 6th of last month.

Rugao 97

Daughter-in-Law Swallows Opium and Kills Herself After Being Humiliated by Mother-in-Law: Wu, the wife of Chen Da of Fanzhuang Township, Libao District, is naturally fierce. After she had a son, San Suo, she hired a matchmaker last year to marry a Shi girl from the Ding family as his wife. She was considered virtuous and the couple got along well. A few days ago, Wu was dissatisfied with something and quarreled with her daughter-in-law, subjecting her to great humiliation. In anger, the daughter-in-law swallowed opium in the night and killed herself. By the time her husband realized it, her life was already gone, and there was no way to bring her back to life.

Ningbo 98

Fire Breaks Out in Yantiwa Lane, Jiangdong: At Xin Yuanjia's house, number 23, Yantiwa Lane, Jiangdong, at around 10:00 PM yesterday afternoon, a fire suddenly broke out. Various fire brigades and carriage teams arrived on the scene to put out the fire. Due to the drought and water shortage, it took over an hour to extinguish the fire. The five rooms and one lane of the building where Xin lived were completely destroyed, with losses estimated at over 3,000 yuan.

Granddaughter-in-Law Chops Ninety-Year-Old Great-Grandfather to Death: Li Guoan, a farmer from the Shanmen area of Zhenhai, has a daughter named Ruixian, who is only seventeen years old and has a sinister nature. She was betrothed to a certain He, but Ruixian disliked her husband's ugly appearance and the couple often quarreled. One day, He returned from outside and spoke sweet words, intending to please his wife. Unexpectedly, Ruixian stabbed her husband with a needle, hitting He's eye and causing him to faint on the ground. As a result, Ruixian left. Since then, no matchmakers have come to her door. Zhang Xiaoyuan from Huangshimen, Shibei Township, had an adopted son. Hearing that Guoan had a daughter, he asked a matchmaker to arrange a marriage and betrothed her as a daughter-in-law. After passing through the door, Ruixian's old nature did not change. One day, Ruixian was in the back door, holding a kitchen knife and cutting vegetables, muttering to herself, filled with resentment. Her husband's grandfather, A San, was ninety-four years old, bent over, and came along tottering. Upon seeing Ruixian, he scolded her harshly, which aroused Ruixian's anger. She swung the kitchen knife in her hand and chopped him, hitting A San's brain. A San was old and lost too much blood and died in less than three hours.

Wang's Father and Son Kidnapped in Shangwang Village: Wang Huaicheng, a resident of Shangwang Village, Yinnan, is a farmer by trade and has a relatively comfortable life, which has attracted the attention of bandits. Yesterday night, more than twenty bandits suddenly came to Wang Renbao's house, a mat merchant in Bishui Village, and forced their way in, claiming to be rice harvesters and asking if he wanted to hire them to harvest rice. Renbao, seeing the situation was not good, escaped through the back door. The bandits then went to Shangwang Village and kidnapped the farmer Wang Huaicheng and his son.

Taizhou 99

Banditry Rages in Tongshu Mountain: Li Changhai, a bandit leader from Dongxiang, Linhai, has gathered more than sixty followers with complete firearms and is gathering in the Tongshu Mountain area of this township, kidnapping people for ransom. Banditry is rampant, and local residents are very panicked. The headquarters of the Fifth Regiment of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Team, stationed in Haimen, has received a report and has dispatched a large team to suppress them. However, the terrain there is dangerous, and it is unknown whether they will be able to eliminate them.

Educational News

Important News

Chen Bulei, Director of the Zhejiang Education Department, Resigns 100

Comes to Shanghai for Medical Treatment Last Night to Show His Resolve

Chen Bulei, a member of the Zhejiang Provincial Government and Director of the Education Department, has strived to maintain and gradually expand educational funding since taking office, at a time when educational funding has been extremely scarce. Previously, due to his weak health, he once submitted a request to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education to resign from his position as Director of the Zhejiang Education Department. However, the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education made every effort to retain him, and he cancelled his resignation. It is now known that Chen is suffering from illness and urgently needs long-term recuperation, so he has once again submitted a request to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education to resign and request that another capable person be appointed to replace him. The Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education believe that Chen has achieved considerable success in handling educational administration in Zhejiang. Although Chen has requested to resign due to illness, it is difficult to find a suitable successor for the time being, so they have repeatedly telegraphed him to earnestly retain him. However, Chen is eager to break free and take the opportunity to recuperate, so his determination to resign is unwavering. He took the train to Shanghai last night for medical treatment and may have to go to Beijing in the near future to personally request his resignation.

International Amateur Athletic Federation 101

Officially Approves New World Records

Opens Divisional Games in Europe, America, and the Far East, National News Agency, Los Angeles, August 8: The International Amateur Athletic Federation met here today and officially approved the numerous new world records and Olympic records set at this year's games. At the same time, it voted to reconsider the case of not recognizing the amateur status of Finnish athletic star Paavo Nurmi (i.e., Normi) at a meeting to be held in Stockholm, Sweden, in August 1934. In addition, it was decided to change the Olympic rules to allow international divisional games to be held before the World Games. One divisional game each may be held in Europe, America, and the Far East.

(1) Women's 100-Meter Freestyle Final

Ms. Madison Breaks Meet Record

Dentsu News, Los Angeles, August 8 - The results of the women's 100-meter freestyle swimming final are as follows:

First: Madison (USA) - 1 minute 6.8 seconds (New Olympic Record)

Second: Terguden (Netherlands)

Third: Xavier (USA)

Fourth: Markham (USA)

Fifth: Prude (Australia)

Sixth: Magal (South Africa)

Los Angeles, August 8 - The winner of the women's 100-meter freestyle swimming final, Ms. Helen Madison (USA), is the world's top female swimmer. Ms. Madison currently holds 16 world records and 53 American records, which is truly astonishing. Today's new meet record broke the 1 minute 11-second record set by Ms. Osborne in the 1928 Games, but failed to surpass her own world-recognized record of 1 minute 6.6 seconds set in 1931. Ms. Madison is currently studying at Lincoln High School and is 19 years old.

Dentsu News, Los Angeles, August 8 - The results of today's water mountain competition are as follows:

Germany won 7 to Brazil 3

Due to the above results, the victory belonged to Hungary. Therefore, the Brazilian team is now banned from participating in water polo competitions.

Jinan University Law School Students' Protection Movement 124

Oppose Merger with Central University

Since the Executive Yuan decided to abolish the Law and Education Schools of the National Jinan University in this city, the students of the school have unanimously opposed it and actively protected the school. Recently, it was reported that student representatives went to Beijing to petition, but without results. The students of the Law School are eager to protect the school and do not want to transfer to Central University, so they organized a school protection movement to demand that the school authorities keep the Law School permanently independent.

Recent News from Jiangwan Yuqing Middle School 125

Since the Shanghai War, Jiangwan Yuqing Middle School has continued to hold classes in temporary school buildings on Connaught Road in the British Concession. Although the school suffered losses, thanks to the efforts of Principal Wang Buxian, the school affairs have continued without interruption. It has now been registered with the Municipal Education Bureau and has moved back to its original site, with classes scheduled to begin on September 1st.

Finance 127

Speculative Gold Reversal and Plunge 128

Sharp Drop of More Than Twelve Taels

Yesterday, speculative gold suddenly reversed direction, with a dramatic decline. However, the market conditions were complex, with frequent fluctuations of two or three taels. In total, the daily range was about six and a half taels. Afterwards, there was a sharp drop of more than twelve taels, with divergent buying and selling and confused intentions among industry players. Ultimately, the market was weak. Silver prices saw a decline in London and an increase in New York, the opposite of the previous day. Futures silver prices surged, so the opening price immediately broke through 740 taels. Subsequently, with the short covering by Yifeng, Hengxing, and others, it reached a high. However, due to the unusual easing of foreign exchange, both the official and unofficial rates for the US dollar increased, and there were always sellers in the market, so the price fell again to 1.45 taels. Later, selling pressure intensified, and with the further strengthening of drafts, it continued to fall by three or four taels, finally settling at only 734 taels, with a pessimistic outlook for the market. The detailed course of the market before and after will now be recorded below.

Opening Plunge of 8.8 Taels

The September futures opened with a sharp drop of 8.8 taels to 737.3 taels. Although large bars fell by one-eighth, the price of American silver unexpectedly rose by one-eighth. The market was unstable, and there were continuous purchases from the United States, which further increased by 7/16 via private telegram. As a result, there were many sellers, and the market sentiment was extremely depressed. Subsequently, due to purchases from Guangbang Hengxing Yifeng and Yifeng Yongda Decheng Hengchang Yong Tong Taichang Heng Yuanyuan and others, the price increased by more than one tael to 39 taels. However, foreign speculators, such as Joe Joseph, sold, causing the price to drop by two taels to 37 taels. As the exchange rate eased, near-term rates were 30 yuan and far-term rates were 30.5 yuan. Then, Mai Bank absorbed 125 for September, Meifeng absorbed 4375 for November, and 25 for October. Yingjin HSBC and others bought 9375 for October. Moreover, the buying pressure in the market suddenly increased, with Hengxing Yifeng Hengxing Yuan Zhaofeng Chang Fuyu Heng Yu Hongkang Yong and others successively pulling in, so the price suddenly surged by more than three taels, reaching 40 taels and 4 qian at 9:30 AM. HSBC quoted British at par and American up 125, at 40 taels and 1 qian. Subsequently, the price increased by two or three qian. Ruixing Hengxing Yuan Yifeng Yong Hongkang Yong Zhifeng Yongyuan Kangxiang and others saw a surge in selling, causing the price to fall sharply by more than four taels to 36 taels. Before long, Yifeng Hengxing Yuan Qianchang Xiangyuan Maoyong Hengchang Yong Hengxing and others entered again and again. In August, US dollars could be sold at 0625, and Meifeng absorbed the November first order at nine pence. At 11 o'clock, the price was 39 taels, (only fluctuating by one tael from 10 o'clock to 11 o'clock). Afterwards, the situation deteriorated, with Hengyu Zhaofeng Chang Hengxing Yuan Hongkang Yong Futai Heng Fuyu Yuantai and other goods sets showing rampant selling pressure. Especially with the near-term first order being able to settle at 8125, US dollars at 0625, and Shanghai offering 30.5 yuan for far-term, McGillivary entered at 625. As a result, the price of gold could not stand firm, falling by three or four taels. It hovered slightly by one or two taels, and finally closed at 35.5 taels at noon. After a while, Yifeng came in, so the closing price was 6 taels and 7 qian, and it was made to 8 taels again. Then, the market sentiment was fluctuating and helpless.

Afternoon Selling Pressure Prevails

The afternoon market opened at 37.3 taels, then at 8.1 taels. Holland absorbed the October British gold at nine pence, and British entered 9375 for September. Later, the American merchant did 1875 for August, and Shanghai offered 375 for October. Also, Fuxing Yong Tong Taichang Hengxing Yuan Hengyu all offered 36.6 taels at 2:30, then added one tael and then fell by more than three taels, because Fuchang Fuyu Hengchang Yong Hengxing Yuan Zhaofeng Chang and others sold vigorously. As the exchange rate became particularly strong, with Mai Bank offering 191875 for November British gold, and the US dollar far-term at 30 yuan and 75, it was not easy to sell. At 3:10 PM, the price was 34 taels and 2 qian, then it increased by one tael to 5 taels and 3 qian, with retail investors coming in. After 3:30 PM, the market situation was ultimately difficult to improve. Bingxing Zhaofeng Chang Hongkang Yong Fuyu and others worked hard to sell. Near the closing time, it finally reached 33 taels and 9 qian. Then, at 4 o'clock, the closing price was 34 taels, falling more than 12 taels and 1 qian compared to the previous day. However, after the close, it rose to 4 taels, 7 or 8 qian. According to the largest price in a day, 40 taels and 4 qian, and the smallest price, 33 taels and 9 qian, there was a difference of 6 taels and a half. The red bar was calculated to increase by eight and a half taels.

Call Prices Mostly Suppressed by Ten Taels

The call price was changed to 807 taels, which was quoted at 125 taels, with a tap of 67, 8 taels to 71 taels, and 73 taels in the afternoon, which was about ten taels more than the previous day. The registered amount was 37 taels, the water compensation was 35 taels, and the after-market was 32 taels.

Transactions at Various Firms Were Extremely Chaotic

Transactions on the table were quite smooth, but each followed its own path, and it was chaotic and at a loss. It is calculated that Guangbang and Yifeng covered short positions of more than 1,000 bars, Hengxing more than 500 bars, Yuan Kangxiang and Zhaofeng Chang entered and then exited, Bingxing Zhifengyong Qianchangxiang Yifengyong Yuanyong Shunli all entered, Tongtaichang Hengxingyuan Hengyu and Fuyu had a lot of deposits and withdrawals, Hengchangyong entered more than 1,000 bars, Ruixing traded on behalf of Joe Joseph and Hongkangyong Yuantai and Futaiheng Yongfeng all exited. In the afternoon, Tongtaichang Dadecheng Qianchangxiang Yifeng and Yongfeng all entered, Yuanyong Zhifengyong Wanxing Hongkangyong entered and then exited, Hengxingyuan Fuxingyong Hengyu Zhaofengchang Yuanheng Bingxing Fuyu all exited, Yuantai Futaiheng Yuanchun Togyurui alternately entered and exited, and Daliangbang sold a total of two or three hundred bars and bought three or four hundred bars. Shandong Province: (1) There has been a large amount of rain in Linqing recently, and the plants are developing well. The cotton plants are as tall as one foot and are in full bloom. Local News

The Heads of Various Ministries of the Executive Yuan

Telegraphed to Nanjing and Luoyang Yesterday to Offer Collective Resignation, Song Ziwen Said the Responsible Cabinet Should Advance and Retreat Together. A Certain Important Person Said the Collective Resignation Was an Active Attempt to Persuade Wang, Wang Jingwei's Attitude was Firm, Entered the Hospital to Recuperate, Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei's Resignation Intentions were Unusually Determined. The previous night he moved to the hospital to rest and refused to meet any guests. Song Ziwen and He Yingqin both visited yesterday morning, but Wang was not there, and they could not meet him. After discussions among the heads of various ministries and commissions, based on the spirit of the responsible cabinet system, they should advance and retreat together with Wang, so they

Wang's Determination to Re-enter Hospital 151

Wang Jingwei's determination to resign this time was unusually firm. At 7:30 PM the previous night, after meeting with various key figures, he left his residence again to recuperate in the hospital. Yesterday, various key figures visited Wang in an endless stream, but none were able to meet him. Song Ziwen and He Yingqin visited at 9:40 AM. Chen Shaokuan went to pay his respects at 11:00 AM. Huang Shaoxiong, accompanied by Li Jishen, went in the afternoon at 3:00 PM. All were told by the gatekeeper that Mr. Wang was out and had not returned, and they left without a meeting. The location of the hospital where Wang was staying was kept a secret from Wang's residence. According to investigations, he is still staying at the Noyer Hospital on Avenue Joffre. Apparently, Wang's diabetes has not yet been completely cured, so he took the opportunity to stay in the hospital for treatment.

Song, He, Zhu, and Others Hustle to Confer 152

Yesterday morning, after Song Ziwen and He Yingqin visited Wang and failed to meet him, they went together to Zhu Peide's residence on Rue Pichon. Because Zhu had not yet arrived in Shanghai, Song returned to his residence. Soon, Zhu Jia骅 and Chen Shaokuan went together to Song's residence to discuss ways to keep Song. At 5:00 PM in the afternoon, Mayor Wu Tiecheng and Zhu Jia骅 and others returned to Song's residence to discuss and exchange opinions. The ministers strongly advocated retaining Wang, saying that as the national crisis was pressing, it was not appropriate to change the central leadership rashly.

Cabinet Ministers Submit Collective Resignation 153

This time, Wang's resignation was resolute, leaving no room for retention. Therefore, the heads of various central ministries and commissions, as the leading figures of the responsible cabinet, having firmly resigned, also submitted their collective resignations yesterday to show their solidarity. The original telegram was sent yesterday afternoon, and the transcribed content is as follows: To the Nanjing Central Political Council, to Chairman Lin in Luoyang, I have received President Wang's telegram. Ziwen and others have been ordered to serve as Vice President, Ministers, and Committee Chairmen of the Executive Yuan. Originally, we hoped to serve to the best of our ability under the leadership of President Wang during the national crisis. Now that President Wang has expressed his resignation, Ziwen and others will naturally resign together. We respectfully request approval of our resignations, with utmost anticipation. Song Ziwen, Huang Shaoxiong, Luo Wengan, He Yingqin, Chen Shaokuan, Zhu Jia骅, Chen Gongbo, Gu Mengyu, Liu Ruiheng, Shi Qingyang, Chen Shuren, respectfully.

The Process of Sending Out the Collective Resignation Telegram 154

The collective resignation telegram jointly submitted by the heads of various ministries and commissions of the Executive Yuan and President Wang's resignation telegram came as a sudden surprise. There was almost no prior indication. It was not until the announcement that it was like a bolt from the blue, causing a stir. However, according to inquiries made by reporters to foreign sources, it was learned that the aforementioned telegrams of collective resignation by the various ministers should have been sent out the day after Wang's resignation telegram was sent. However, initially, because some ministers were not in Shanghai, according to the law, Vice President Song should lead the list. On the morning of the 7th, after the draft of the telegram was finalized, it was telegraphed to various ministers to seek their consent. After the replies from all parties were received, it was already in the evening of the 7th. The secretary transcribed the telegram and recorded the names of the various ministers before handing the transcribed draft to Song, Zhu, and others for review (Minister of Education Zhu Jia骅 was also at Song's residence at the time). While awaiting publication, Mayor Wu Tiecheng and Vice President Yang Xingfo of the Academia Sinica were also present. Upon seeing the draft telegram, Wu immediately stood up and strongly advised against sending it, saying that if the collective resignation telegram were published at this time, the situation would inevitably become more serious, and the public would inevitably feel more anxious. The Shanghai financial market might be disrupted. For the sake of stabilizing public sentiment and taking the overall situation into account, it should be postponed. Moreover, there was sincere persuasion to retain Mr. Wang, and there might be hope of reversing the situation. Why not delay it for a while, and so on. Although Song and Zhu thought it was reasonable, they felt that since the entire responsibility was involved, the ministers should resign together without hesitation. They were just about to explain to Wu when a written message from Wang arrived, inviting the ministers in Shanghai (in addition to Song and Zhu, there were also Huang Shaoxiong, Zeng Zhongming, etc.) to meet at Wang's residence on the morning of the 8th. Wu Tiecheng thus held even more firmly to the proposal to delay the telegram. Song and others also felt that there was a turning point, and it seemed that it could be delayed slightly. The telegram was thus left at Song's residence. At the meeting on the morning of the 8th, Song, Zhu, and others unanimously represented the central government in retaining Wang, and the results were quite good. Therefore, the telegram was not published again. However, yesterday, Wang re-entered the hospital to avoid noise and declined to see guests. Song and others had no choice but to send out the telegram, but it had been delayed for two days from the original intention. According to the recent central political system, the Executive Yuan is equivalent to a responsible cabinet. Therefore, when the President of the Yuan retires due to the complexity of government affairs, the heads of the various ministries and commissions under the Executive Yuan should naturally resign together. This is a necessary procedure in the government's organization. Therefore, after Wang sent out his resignation telegram on the 6th, Song and others, upon receiving the news, immediately drafted a telegram in preparation for a collective resignation, to show a unified step and a unified action. If there had been no consideration for the overall situation, this telegram would have been published on the 7th. Therefore, the text of the telegram is still the original text from two days ago, which is very brief. As for the various ministries and commissions after the collective resignation, they will continue to work as usual, and the ministries will continue to be responsible for their work, without any stagnation, only preparing to hand over at any time. This preparation will also be lifted when Wang returns to his post.

Mr. Song Ziwen's Statement 155

Mr. Song Ziwen made a statement yesterday regarding the collective resignation of the heads of various ministries and commissions, saying that no one on any side knew beforehand about Mr. Wang's coming to Shanghai to resign. However, since the Executive Yuan was changed to a responsible cabinet system after the First Plenary Session, and Mr. Wang has expressed his resignation, the administration has lost its leadership. The heads of the various ministries and commissions should naturally resign together. This is the common practice of the responsible cabinet system in various countries, and it is a necessary expression of solidarity for those who bear political responsibility. There are no other reasons. As for the administrative affairs of the various ministries and commissions, during the period when the government has not appointed replacements, colleagues will naturally continue to be responsible.

Chen Shaokuan Declares His Determination to Resign 156

Regarding the collective resignation of the heads of various central ministries and commissions, a reporter specially interviewed Navy Minister Chen Shaokuan yesterday. According to Chen, the central authorities have not yet approved this resignation. If President Wang can indeed withdraw his resignation, he will still resign from his post as Navy Minister. The central authorities are still actively trying to retain President Wang. This morning, he and Minister Song, Minister Zhu, and others are still discussing ways to retain him. As for the rumors that the President of the Central Executive Yuan will be re-elected within a few days, he has not heard of them. As for the issue of Zhang Xueliang's resignation, he does not know whether the central authorities will approve it because he is in Shanghai, and it has not been discussed in Shanghai.

Collective Resignation is an Active Effort to Retain Wang 157

A certain key government figure told reporters yesterday that everyone is making every effort to retain the resignation of Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan. It is too early to talk about the reorganization of the National Government at this time. The collective resignation of the heads of various ministries and commissions is actually a new way to actively retain Wang. Moreover, the current President of the Executive Yuan is equivalent to the Prime Minister of the cabinet in various countries, and the ministers are all cabinet members. When the Prime Minister resigns, the cabinet members naturally advance and retreat with him. The question of whether or not to approve Zhang Xueliang's resignation is also under consideration and a solution will be found soon.

Wang's Announcement in Response to Various Groups 158

In response to the letters of encouragement and reprimand from various groups in Shanghai, Wang specially issued an announcement, saying, "To the various circles of Shanghai: In recent days, I have received letters from various circles regarding Zhaoming's resignation, either earnestly urging me to stay or severely reprimanding me. I have received them all. The reasons for Zhaoming's resignation have been detailed in my telegram to Director Zhang and in my joint telegram to the Central Executive Committee. I will not repeat them one by one. I hereby reply briefly, and I hope you will understand. Wang Zhaoming, respectfully, August 9th."

Wu Zhihui Also Firmly Advocates Retaining Wang 159

A reporter from the East China News Agency visited Central Committee Member Wu Zhihui yesterday and asked about the resignations of Wang Jingwei and Zhang Xueliang. According to Wu, he visited Mr. Wang the day before yesterday, not to retain him, but to understand Mr. Wang's intention to resign. Currently, most parties advocate retaining Mr. Wang, but Mr. Wang's intention to resign is indeed very firm. However, his resignation is not passive, because Mr. Wang stated that if the central government could approve his resignation, he would still return to Beijing to serve. Therefore, if the central government approves Mr. Wang's resignation, it will not have an impact on the political situation. As for his successor, Mr. Wang advocates that Cai Yuanpei, Yu Youren, and Dai Jitao take over. I also think it is appropriate. As for Zhang Xueliang's resignation, because I am in Shanghai, I do not know whether the central government will approve it. However, based on my understanding, Zhang Xueliang is not foolish. Having lost the position of little emperor of the three northeastern provinces due to non-resistance, he is confined to being a little emperor of Beiping. The Japanese invaders are encroaching step by step, yet there is still no sign of resistance. This may be due to other diplomatic relations. We should now understand why the Northeast Volunteer Army is so active outside the customs, and the Japanese hate Zhang so much. Why did the 19th Route Army and the 5th Army resist the Japanese in Shanghai, and Chairman Chiang of the Military Affairs Commission did not want to add the name of resistance to himself? Why? We should use strength as a backing on the one hand, but also use diplomacy on the other. There are three major trends in the world today: red imperialism, white imperialism, and fascism. Red imperialism is, of course, the Soviet Union. White imperialism is led by the United Kingdom and the United States. Fascism originated in Italy, and Japan has now succeeded, and Germany is also booming. The three major trends in the world cannot cooperate at all. Japan's fascism has succeeded by swallowing up the eastern provinces, but white imperialists are very unwilling to see Japan swallowing up the eastern provinces. They do not want fascism to be the leader of East Asia. Therefore, they express great anger at Japan's annexation of the eastern provinces in terms of international morality. But their diplomatic skills are very cautious and they do not act rashly. They want to slowly make Japan gradually vomit out the eastern provinces it has already swallowed, but at the same time they are unwilling to immediately help China, so that China can shake off its shackles and retaliate by abolishing unequal treaties. Therefore, they hesitate and are still not fully and clearly expressed. Therefore, many Chinese people would rather be followers of redism. China is in the midst of these three major trends, and the authorities must be very cautious in their diplomacy. Zhang Xueliang may not be able to fully express himself due to diplomatic relations, and his childlike temper is especially prone to offending people.

Mi Chunlin Scheduled to Leave Shanghai in a Week 160

Mi Chunlin, Zhang Xueliang's representative, has visited Mayor Wu and Finance Minister Song since arriving in Shanghai the day before yesterday, personally delivering Zhang Xueliang's letters. According to him, the purpose of his visit to Shanghai was to meet with Mr. Wang to explain everything, but there has been no opportunity to meet with Mr. Wang. Zhang Xueliang also has a personal letter to Mr. Wang explaining the situation in North China. After visiting Wang, I will earnestly ask Mr. Wang to withdraw his resignation. His stay in Shanghai is expected to be about a week.

Ma Ze Zhao 161

Yesterday's Reception for the Press 162

Report on the Current Situation of Negotiations between Kang and Tibet. Ma Ze Zhao, representative of the people of Xikang and director of the resident Beijing office, specially came to Shanghai from Beijing on the 7th to make the people of the whole country understand the situation in Kang and Tibet, unite to eliminate foreign troubles, and consolidate national defense. Yesterday, at the Eastern Hotel on Tibet Road, he hosted the local press to report everything. Dozens of reporters from various newspapers attended. Ma's report is recorded below:

Mr. Ma said, "Today, I am very honored that the Shanghai press, which bears the important mission of arousing public opinion and urging the government, has come here. What I am prepared to report to you is the Kang-Tibet incident, which has not been paid attention to by the people in the country and is now extremely serious, that is, the national defense incident in southwestern China. In the 19th year of the Republic, I was elected by all the people of Tibet to serve as a people's representative in Beijing. Recently, I have been aware of the seriousness of the situation in Kang and Tibet, the urgency of national defense, and the lack of understanding of the Kang affairs among the people in the country. In order to make the people of the whole country understand the situation in Kang and Tibet, unite to eliminate foreign troubles, develop resources, and consolidate national defense, I have specially come here from Nanjing to give you a brief report, in order to obtain powerful assistance and instruction. It is divided into four points: (1) The status of Xikang, externally connected with Tibet under the Dalai Lama's yellow lion flag, internally connected with the provinces of Sichuan, Yunnan, and Qinghai. In the third year of the Republic, the northern government unified the administrative regions and designated Kangding as the first capital. The eastern part of Kangding was settled, and the rest of the southern road was thirteen counties such as Yajiang, Lihua, and Ba'an. The northern road was seven counties such as Daofu and Ganmei. The middle road was four counties such as Zhanhua and Baiyu. Including Jiulong, Danba, and other places, there are a total of thirty-two counties. During the Xinhai Revolution, the Tibetan army took advantage of the rise of our revolutionary army to invade and occupy Sang'ang and Chayu, west of the Lancang River. In the seventh year of the Republic, they also occupied ten counties such as Qamdo and Ningjing. In the 19th year of the Republic, on the pretext of a minor dispute between the Da and Bai temples, they occupied Ganzi, Zhanhua, and Qiongxia of Lihua. The Zhubo and other places in Huo, and unfortunately, the Kang-Tibetan dispute was formed. In total, the Tibetan army occupied about three-quarters of the Kang area. The violence has lasted for more than twenty years, and all miscellaneous grains, butter, tea, salt, horse grass, etc. have been requisitioned from the Kang people. If they do not obey, they will suffer the tragic punishment of amputation and cutting off the nose. The people of Bieli Village could not bear the abuse and migrated to avoid it, wandering and unable to return home. It is painful to say that because it is far away from the center, although the territory has been invaded and the people are in dire straits, the government and the people of the country are still indifferent. The Dalai Lama has another background and is manipulated by others, and has no sincerity towards the central government. This can be seen from the historical facts. In the dispute between the Da and Bai temples two years ago, it was a minor incident. The Tibetan side sided with Dajie Temple, used it as an excuse to attack our Kang defense army, and at the same time sent a message to the central government, asking to send personnel for peaceful mediation. At the same time, they sent troops to occupy Ganzi and Zhanhua. After the central special envoy Tang Kesan arrived in Kang, he saw that they had other conspiracies and could not mediate. Peace was hopeless, so he had to leave Kang and return to Beijing. The Kang affairs became deadlocked. In April of this year, the Tibetan army suddenly advanced in three routes to attack our army. Our army was forced to counterattack and advanced to recover Ganzi. On the 7th day of July, the enemy counterattacked again and was repelled by our army, and Dajie Temple was captured again, and advanced to Rongba, Chayu, and other places. Recently, Kang received a telegram that the Dalai Lama was angry at the defeat on the front line. On the one hand, he transported a large number of new weapons purchased from abroad to the front line to replenish them. On the other hand, he mobilized the entire Tibetan army to launch a full-scale counterattack, and the Dalai Lama personally went to Qamdo to command, attempting to recapture Ganzhan in one fell swoop and occupy the entire Kang. This is the Dalai Lama's unrighteous infringement of national defense. (2) Since the Tibetan side started the war again, this office has repeatedly received Kang telegrams, saying that the Tibetan army has airplanes, cannons, and other items in this battle, and all kinds of new weapons should be available. The people of Kang have repeatedly telegraphed and requested the central government to provide assistance with national strength. After this office repeatedly submitted and requested the central government to quickly determine a major plan to strengthen national defense, it was heard that the central government is still under planning. As for the allocation of ammunition, the Ministry of Military Affairs promised to temporarily allocate some bullets to provide assistance. At present, the war situation in the front line is not only urgent in the northern road, but the Tibetan army is also disturbing Ba'an, and the southern road is also tense at the same time. Recently, the Kang border defense army Commander Yu sent a letter, saying that the north and south roads are requesting reinforcements and ammunition, and the urgent requests are constant. It is extremely difficult for the isolated army to cope with it on both sides. It seems that the war zone has expanded and the consumption has increased, which is impossible without the central government's full assistance. The climate in Kang is cold in autumn. Now that summer is over, winter will arrive in a blink of an eye. The military needs extremely urgent supplies such as leather shoes and leather vests to keep out the cold. This office is now actively requesting the government, on the one hand, to implement the policy of recovering Xikang, continue to use force to drive out the Tibetan bandits, and on the other hand, to provide full assistance with ammunition and expenses, so as to avoid the isolated army fighting hard and being difficult to support. (3) Xikang is not the Xikang of the people of Xikang, nor is it the Xikang of Liu Zongzhihui Wenhui. In other words, it is not the provincial defense of a certain province, but the national defense of the entire Republic of China. How to plan and handle it as a whole should be decided by the central government and handed over to the border defense officers in charge. It cannot be blamed on a certain person to resist with the strength of a corner of the country. This battle is purely for saving the people of Kang and consolidating national defense, which is different from internal wars. The Dalai Lama's military action is for tigers to be slaves, for people to be puppets. Those who suffer are directly the insignificant Kang people, and indirectly the manifestation of imperialism attacking our entire nation. With the loss of the Northeast, the balance of power of the imperialists in the Far East has already been lost. If the people of the country do not take precautions against the Kang and Tibet coveted by a certain country, I dare to say that in the near future, it will be the second Northeast. For the sake of prevention, now we should take advantage of this victory and the high morale, and the central government should immediately order Chairman Liu to continue to advance victoriously and recover all lost lands. On the one hand, we should fully provide assistance with ammunition and expenses, and hold them responsible for success, recover Xikang, engage in construction, and then plan to reform Tibet. Otherwise, even if we win by luck, the Tibetan army will inevitably take the opportunity to occupy Xikang again. This office's work is now focused on this, and I hope that our enlightened press will give us assistance, then Xikang will be fortunate, and national defense will be fortunate. (4) Xikang's production, such as mines, forests, animal husbandry, and medicinal materials, are extremely abundant, but they have not been developed. It is like a treasure house, which is still locked and has not been opened. If a large amount of capital can be invested to develop it, the good results will be like a sure thing. Shanghai is the center of capital concentration in our country. I hope that you will actively promote and urge the attention of all walks of life to invest and develop, which will be greatly beneficial to the national economy and the people's livelihood. On behalf of the people of Kang, I extend my sincere hope to you, and I offer a glass and wish you all good health.

The Kang-Tibetan War, the Kang-Tibetan War, has recently become more intense again. Mr. Shi received a telegram from Yu Songlin, the commander-in-chief of Xikang, reporting on the recent war situation. The original telegram is recorded below: "To Mr. Ma Zezhao, Director of the Xikang Resident Beijing Office: After our army captured Dajin Yulong, the Tibetan side took advantage of the fact that we were focusing on local settlement and had no time to advance to counterattack with reinforcements. Since the 25th, our army has fought on three routes, which has been very fierce. Finally, on the 27th, we occupied Keludong, and on the 28th, we recovered Dege County. On the 29th, we went straight to Gangtuo River ferry on the Jinsha River. The Tibetan army mostly crossed the river westward. The Tibetan troops in Dengke, Shiqu, Baiyu, and other counties heard that Dege had been captured by our army and were preparing to retreat to the west bank of the Jinsha River. We are sending troops to recover them. On the 25th, we sent the Ma regiment from Lihua to Ba'an to take over the defense. The areas lost in the seventh year of the Republic can be fully recovered within days. However, in each battle, the wounded officers and soldiers have consumed a lot of bullets. The headquarters has stopped various miscellaneous expenses for the border war, so it is difficult to prepare military supplies and transport food. If this continues, it is really impossible for one army to shoulder this important task of national defense. What will happen in the future? My brother has foresight and vision. I hope you will give me instructions. Yours sincerely, Winter."

Japanese Troops Stationed in Shanghai 165

Continued Increase of Over Two Thousand Troops Daily 166

It is reported by the Shiwenshe that the existing garrison had already reached over three thousand two hundred men. According to reliable sources, the Commander of the Third Fleet of the Japanese Navy stationed in Shanghai, Sakonji, and the Commander of the Marine Corps, Sugisaka, have repeatedly telegraphed the Naval Ministry, requesting additional naval personnel to be sent to Shanghai. In the past week alone, over two thousand three hundred Japanese naval personnel have been dispatched to Shanghai. The various pieces of information obtained by the Shiwenshe reporter are recorded below:

Japanese troops are continuously increasing in Shanghai. After the formal signing of the armistice agreement, the Japanese regular army and naval landing forces stationed in Shanghai were ordered to withdraw to their home country in batches. The majority of them were immediately transferred to Guanwai (Northeast China) to join the Japanese army in fighting against the volunteer forces. Up until around the 20th of last month, the Japanese Navy in Shanghai consisted of only over eight hundred and forty special marine corps members, eight hundred stationed at the Japanese Naval Headquarters on Jiangwan Road, and over forty stationed at the Toyota Textile Mill in western Shanghai. Since the Northeast Customs was seized and the Chinese government decided to levy tariffs on goods transported to the Northeast, Japanese merchants in Shanghai have been requesting the Commander of the Third Fleet of the Navy, Sakonji, to protect cargo transportation by force. Recently, the activities of the Blood Soul Assassination Corps have dealt a major blow to Japanese trade with China. Commander Sakonji and Commander of the Marine Corps Sugisaka, deeply concerned that the military strength in Shanghai was insufficient to meet the needs of overseas merchants, repeatedly telegraphed the Japanese Naval Ministry, requesting additional naval personnel to be sent to Shanghai to assist in managing affairs. As of yesterday (the 8th), in addition to the original eight hundred men stationed at the Japanese Naval Headquarters on Jiangwan Road, four new battalions of marines, approximately two thousand eight hundred and eighty men, newly dispatched from the home country, have been stationed. At the same time, three platoons of Japanese soldiers, totaling approximately two hundred and forty men, have been stationed at the Dobun Shoin Academy and Toyota Textile Mill in western Shanghai. In total, over the past week, over two thousand three hundred Japanese naval personnel have been dispatched from the home country to Shanghai. Combined with the original troops in Shanghai, the actual number is confirmed to be over three thousand one hundred men. According to the Japanese Navy's organization in Shanghai, three companies form a battalion, three platoons form a company, and each platoon has eighty men. Currently, the Japanese troops in Shanghai consist of a total of four battalions and three platoons.

Sugisaka Strictly Establishes Training Regulations. Sugisaka, Commander of the Japanese Naval Marine Corps, considering the increasing number of naval personnel stationed in Shanghai, has strictly re-established the previously established training rules for the sake of unified training. It is stipulated that if the temperature exceeds ninety degrees, afternoon training will be suspended, but in the morning, soldiers must still rise at five o'clock, practice street fighting tactics for two hours, and academic subjects for one hour. If the temperature does not exceed ninety degrees, all must attend two training sessions in the afternoon. It is also stipulated that a platoon inspection will be held once a week, and a general review will be held every three weeks. These new training regulations were communicated yesterday to all subordinate officers and soldiers for compliance.

A Portion of Japanese Troops Will Return Home. According to news from the Japanese Naval Headquarters on Jiangwan Road, a portion of the Marine Corps, over three hundred and fifty men, will be returning home on the Tenryu Maru on the 9th. The date of departure has not yet been determined. However, according to another source, the three hundred and fifty men being transferred home will be sent to Guanwai to assist in the attack on Jehol.

For the sake of caution, an emergency meeting of all executive committee members was immediately convened on the 5th of this month. (Resolution) Handle the case together. As an impromptu motion, it was decided that the association's fund should not be used for any administrative expenses, and that the reduction of administrative expenses should still be donated by the members themselves. Local News Two

Ship Sinks Rowboat 182

Rowboat Capsizes, Over Ten People Fall into River

One Female Worker Rescued, Two Bodies Recovered

The Hakone Maru, a European liner of the Japanese Mail Steamship Company, arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong the previous day and docked at the Wayside Wharf. Yesterday morning around 5:00 AM, it departed Shanghai for Japan. While turning around to exit, its propellers sank a sampan, resulting in fatalities. The details of the incident are recorded as follows:

The Hakone Maru, having arrived in Shanghai from Europe, docked at the Hongkou Wayside Wharf to load and unload cargo. It began to weigh anchor for Japan at 5:45 AM yesterday morning. Tugs were used to tow and maneuver the ship, including a turn. At that time, the tide was rising rapidly. According to usual practice, when turning with the rising tide, the stern of the ship had to be towed towards Pudong before the bow could be steered outwards. As the tugboats were towing the stern towards Pudong, a sampan, fully loaded with female workers on their way from Qichang Wharf to work in Puxi, was passing by the stern of the Hakone Maru. Seeing the ship stationary, the sampan attempted to pass quickly. Unexpectedly, the propellers suddenly started, creating a surge of waves that immediately sank the small sampan, causing all ten-plus people on board to completely submerge.

When the sampan was hit and sank, cries for help were incessant, but due to the large size of the ship, the immense power of its engines, and the waves several feet high, nearby boats did not dare to approach and rescue the drowning victims, and were only able to watch it sink. After the ship moved far away, it was too late to salvage anything. Only one girl was rescued, named Qu Fuying, about twelve years old. When the sampan overturned, she was swept by a wave under the Qichang Wharf. The girl grabbed onto a concrete pillar of the wharf and was then pulled ashore by an elderly man. The girl went home by herself. Later, the Wayside Road Water Police Station investigated and found that after the girl returned home, she became ill due to shock and swallowing several mouthfuls of water, but was not in great danger.

After receiving a report, the Wayside Road Water Police Station dispatched detectives to investigate the scene. They saw the Hakone Maru proceeding as usual. The police took the sampan and its boatmen, Du Jutian and Du Xiaodingzi, both from Jiangbei, back to the police station. At Qichang Wharf, a woman named Wu Yangshi, wife of Wu Zhaohan, was crying, and she was also taken back to the police station. According to Wu Yangshi, she, her daughter Wu Pindi, 13, and her niece Yang Jincui, 16, all worked at the Shenxin No. 7 Factory, and were traveling together to work in Puxi. She herself wanted to go to Shanghai, so she took a city ferry, a small steamer. On the small steamer, she saw the sampan her two daughters were riding in suddenly sink, and knew that her two daughters had drowned. She said that she had given birth to nine children, but eight had already died young, leaving only this one daughter, hoping she could find a son-in-law to rely on in old age. As she spoke, she wept bitterly and was inconsolable. The police chief comforted her and sent her home, telling her that they would notify her when the bodies were recovered so she could identify them.

After bringing the boatmen Du Jutian and Du Xiaodingzi back to the police station, the police chief conducted a preliminary interrogation. They confessed to carrying ten people in total and recounted the details of the incident. The sampan boatmen were temporarily detained at the Water Police Station and were to be sent to the local court for disposition tomorrow morning (i.e., this morning). According to Qu Fuying, who escaped danger, there were about twelve people on the boat at the time. Apart from the report from Wu Pindi's mother, the police station had received no reports from other families, so they assumed that some families were unaware of the situation. Since the bodies had not yet been recovered, the number of victims was not yet confirmed.

After the incident, in addition to the Water Police attempting a salvage operation, a compradore from Qichang Wharf, a Cantonese man, hired small fishing boats to retrieve the bodies, offering three dollars for each one. Around 10:00 AM, a fishing boat belonging to Zhu Da Wangzi recovered a female body, about ten years old, from the nearby Huangpu River. Relatives were present and immediately claimed the body for burial without notifying the police station. Later, at 11:30 AM, another female body, about fifteen years old, named Ni Lindi, was retrieved near the wharf. A patrolman noticed and ordered the fishing boat to send the body to the Water Police Station, which then transported it to the Nanshi Salvation Bureau for temporary storage, awaiting forensic examination by the court tomorrow morning (i.e., this morning).

After the incident, the Hakone Maru believed it was not involved and, due to its scheduled departure, did not offer assistance, departing as scheduled. The ship's officer sent a radio message to the Japanese Mail Steamship Company in Shanghai.

Paramour Gruesomely Murders Mistress 183

Triggered by Woman's Infidelity

Murderer Caught on Scene by Police at 825, Rear Building, Zhang Xiaoquan Scissors Shop, Corner of Seward Road and Dent Road. Murder Case Occurred Yesterday Afternoon; Murderer Caught on Scene. Details as Follows:

"One Cut Severed" Becomes Ominous Prophecy: Murderer Pu Henian, 23, from Qingpu, male; victim Wang Xiuying, 25, from Suzhou, female. They rented a room on the upper floor of the Zhang Xiaoquan Scissors Shop last month on the 19th, agreeing on a monthly rent of six yuan. Pu claimed his surname was Chen and that they were husband and wife, with him being a primary school teacher. The sublessor saw that their behavior was civilized, so they did not investigate their background. Moreover, the two were very close on weekdays, so no suspicion arose. The previous night (the 8th), Xiuying went out and did not return until yesterday morning. When Henian returned home for lunch yesterday afternoon, he immediately questioned her about where she had stayed the previous night. Xiuying replied that she had stayed in a rented room. As a result, the two started arguing. Finally, Xiuying said that since they were not compatible, they might as well "sever with one cut" and ordered Henian to write a separation agreement. At that moment, Pu became uncontrollably angry and declared, "Since you want to 'sever with one cut,' there's a way to do it." He immediately grabbed a kitchen knife from the table and violently slashed Xiuying's face.

Alert Sublessor Raises Alarm: Xiuying was only wearing a short vest and shorts, lying on the bed. After being slashed in the face, she jumped up from the bed and screamed for help. Liu Cao Shi, the sublessor downstairs, was having lunch. Hearing the cries for help, she stopped eating and went upstairs, knocking urgently on the door. Pu did not respond. She crouched down and peeked through the crack in the door, and saw Xiuying rolling around on the floor, screaming in pain, with bloodstains all over the floor. Mrs. Liu realized something had happened and quickly turned around to go downstairs, instructing her apprentice to call the police. Returning upstairs, she saw that Xiuying had died, and Pu Henian was halfway down the stairs, trying to escape. Liu Cao Shi grabbed him. Fortunately, patrolman No. 2023 from a nearby post also arrived after being notified and apprehended the murderer, sending him to the Wayside Police Station. The police station dispatched officers to investigate the scene, and the body was transported by vehicle to the Ferron Road morgue to await examination.

Paramour Refuses Additional Lovers: The murderer Pu Henian confessed at the police station that he made a living selling pills for rejuvenation. The victim Wang Xiuying was his mistress. They met on a Suzhou steamer on March 25 of this year. They first lived in the French Concession. Later, because Pu's legal wife came to Shanghai, they moved to this location. Recently, Xiuying had not been keeping to her duties, frequently staying out. He had found out that she had a relationship with a certain teaboy at the Central Hotel. Her staying out the previous night was because she and the teaboy had been together at a Suzhou hotel. When he questioned her slightly, Xiuying forced him to write a separation agreement, which is why he did it out of anger.

Seven Cuts Sever Left Hand: Wang Xiuying was slashed a total of seven times by Pu Henian. Five cuts were to the head, including two on the throat and three on the eyes, nose, and face. There was one cut on the right shoulder and back. The left hand was cut off and fell to the ground. As a result, blood flowed all over the place. The downstairs area, as well as the bedclothes and other items in the room, were covered with bloodstains. The corpse lay in a pool of blood, a truly gruesome sight that was unbearable to witness.

Raid on Baker Road 184

Lake Region Kidnapping Gang 185

Ten Male and Female Kidnappers Apprehended

Seven Kidnapped Children Rescued

Exotic Prostitute's Madame Also an Accomplice

Chen Yueying's Experienced Ordeal: Recently, the Zhabei Police Station received a secret report stating that a large group of kidnappers was hiding at No. 7 Qunshou Lane, 161 Baker Road, specializing in trafficking women. On the morning of the day before yesterday at 9:25 AM, police chief Nai Pai, along with Chinese detectives Tang Jian, Ding Huaguo, Yang Fusheng, Bao Tan Zhang Yutian, and Western detective Bao Tai, went to investigate. They discovered that the residents of the house were mostly from the Lake Region and used deception to lure girls from their hometowns to Shanghai for sale, profiting from the transactions. The police then began the arrests, apprehending ten male and female kidnappers, including Zhou Cuilan (also known as Lansheng), Tao Guifu, Shen Runliu, Fei Futang, Bi Chengdeng, Tao Guisheng, Zhou Zixiang, and the women Fei Bi Shi, Shen Su Shi, and Tao Yuan Shi, along with sixteen-year-old Fei Xianglin, fifteen-year-old Zhang Baozhu, thirteen-year-old Shi Zhubao, fifteen-year-old Zhou Lanzhen, seventeen-year-old Tao Mao, sixteen-year-old Chen Yueying, and five-year-old boy Zhou Amao, all from the Lake Region. Afterwards, they went to the Yanfei Brothel at No. 323 Huile Lane, Fuzhou Road, and apprehended an accomplice, the Suzhou brothel owner Pan Lao Si, and brought them to the police station. The police chief ordered the eleven male and female defendants to be detained separately. The remaining boys and girls were temporarily sent to the Jiliang Institute for care. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Second Criminal Division of the First Special District Court. The defendants hired three lawyers, Yuan Yang'an, etc., to defend them. According to police lawyer Wang Yaotang, the defendants were prosecuted for the crime of disrupting families under Article 257 of the Criminal Code. He detailed the circumstances of the case, stating that according to the defendant Zhou Cuilan's confession at the police station, she had purchased Zhou Lanzhen and Chen Yueying twelve years ago in the Lake Region, and Chen was placed in the care of Yanfei brothel owner Pan Lao Si. In March of this year, Pan took Chen Yueying to Room 330 of the Grand China Hotel on Xizang Road, where she came to an agreement with Tan Liming (also known as Wu Huadong), a captain in a certain organization in Nanjing. Tan paid 200 yuan to deflower Chen Yueying. The police required more time to investigate this complex case in detail and therefore requested a postponement. Fei Xianglin confessed that she was sixteen years old and from the Lake Region. She had been sold as a servant to the Chen family since she was young. Four days ago, the defendants Fei Futang and Bi Chengrui took her to Shanghai from her village to sell her to Shen Runliu for 240 yuan. They lived on Baker Road. The defendant Bi Chengrui confessed that Fei's owner, Chen, was the owner of the Chen Futai Nanhuo store in Xiaang of the Lake Region, and he had known him for a long time. Recently, Fei Futang asked me to be a matchmaker, so Fei and I brought Fei to Shanghai and stayed overnight at the Hongxiang Hotel. The next day, we went to Baker Road. I asked Fei Chentang because I had a friend, Zhou Songshan, who was an employee of the Tongfeng Nanhuo store in Xiaodongmen. He had recently lost his wife, so he asked me to find a replacement. I then entrusted Bi Chengrui to negotiate with Chen Futai in Xiaang of the Lake Region and agreed to buy Fei Xianglin for 240 yuan. The victim Zhang Baozhu confessed that she was fifteen years old and from the Lake Region. Because of poverty, her mother brought her to Shanghai three weeks ago to work as a servant at Tao Guifu's house on Baker Road. Tao Amao confessed to being from Hangzhou, seventeen years old, and said the defendants Tao Guifu and Tao Yuan Shi were his biological parents. Shi was brought to them by Zhou Cuilan because his mother was recently ill and unable to work, so they hired Shi to help with chores and prepare meals. Presiding Judge Wu Tingqi, after reviewing the confessions, ordered that the defendants be held in custody, that the boys and girls remain in the care of Jiliang, and adjourned the case for further hearing.
